nity─Бtmuс╕Нai yuс╣Зс╕Нi nityuс╕Нai velugondu

─У d─Уvu d─Уhamuna ninniyunu janmi├▒ce
n─У d─Уvu d─Уhamuna ninniyu naс╣Зaс╣Еge mari

23
Who is the Lord from whose body everything emanated ,
Who is the Lord into whose body everything finally merges,
Who is the Lord whose form constitutes everything,
Who is the Lord who has sun and moon as eyes,
Who is the Lord existing within all Jivas,
Who is the Lord whose vitality supports all,
Who is the Lord who is unmanifest,
Who is the Lord who has none as a second?
That Lord is the Lord of Venkatadri!
Who is the God whose feet are the earth and sky,
Who is the God whose entire form is limitless,
Who is the God whose exhalation is the powerful wind,
Who is the God whose true servants are the meritorious ones,
Who is the God who is the ruler of all,
Who is the God existing as the Supreme Overlord,
Who is the God who eternally thinks about the welfare of this world,
Who is the God who is most subtle and also the most extraordinary?
That God is the Lord of Tiru Venkatadri!
─У d─Уvu n─Уtrambu lina candrulu,
─У d─Уvu с╕Н─лj─лvu linniс╣Зс╣нil┼Н nuс╣Зс╕Нu
n─Уd─Уvu caitanya minniс╣нiki n─Бdh─Бra
m─Уd─Уvu с╕Нavyaktuс╕Н─У d─Уvuс╕Нadvandvu
с╕Н─Б d─Уvuс╕Н─л v─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─Бdrivibhuс╕Нu….nity─Б..
─У v─Уlpu p─Бdhayuga milayu n─Бk─Б┼Ыambu
─У v─Уlpu p─Бdak─У ┼Ы─Бntaс╣Г banantambu
─У v─Уlpu ni┼Ыv─Бsa m─л mah─Бm─Бrutamu
─У v─Уlpu nijad─Бsul─л puс╣Зyulu
─У v─Уlpu sarv─У┼Ыuс╕Н─У v─Уlpu param─У┼Ыu
с╕Н─У v─Уlpu bhuvanaika hitaman┼Нbh─Бvakuс╕Нu
─У v─Уlpu kaс╕Нu s┼лkс╣гma m─Уv─Уlpu kaс╕Нu ghanamu
─Б v─Уlpu tiruv─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─Бdrivibhuс╕Нu ….nity─Б..
Being the eternal indweller, shining effulgently as the eternal being,
being the true self, and existing as the truth,
being manifest, and being the Supreme Brahman,
He is the one who is the most adorable, this Lord of Tiru Venkatadri!
Who is the deity who rules over all worlds,
Who is the deity sought by Brahma and others,
Who is the deity who can bestow true salvation,
Who is the deity who is the sole well wisher of the Universe,
Who is the deity who possesses a true form,
Who is the deity who cannot be described in any form,
Who is the deity whose form includes the trinity,
Who is the deity existing as the inner self of all,
Who is the deity who is the Paramatma?
That deity is the Lord of Venkatadri!

рдЖрджрд┐рдордкреВрд░реБрд╖реБ рдбрдЪреНрдпреБрддреБ рдбрдЪрд▓реБ

─Бdimap┼лruс╣гu с╕Нacyutu с╕Нacalu с╕Нanantuс╣Г с╕Нamaluс╕Нu

baikoniyuс╣Зс╕Нaga nokavaс╣нapatramul┼Нpalanu
c─Уkoni pavaс╕╖impucu noka┼Ыi┼Ыuvai vaс╕Нi d─Уl─Бс╕Нina -
┼Ыr─лk─Бntu с╕Н─лtaс╕Н─Уp┼Н ┼Ыr─лv─Ус╣Еkaс╣нavibhuс╕Нu …. ─Бdi ..
aruduga balimada maс╕Нapaga n─Бkasamaс╣Зс╣нinar┼лpamu
sarugana bh┼лmintayu nokacaraс╣Зambuna golaci

kс╣г─лrapay┼Нnidhil┼Нpala ┼Ы─Ус╣гuс╕Нu paryaс╣Еkamug─Б
dh─Бruс╣Зiyanu siriyunu b─Бdamu lottaganu
c─Уruva danu brahm─Бdulu s─Уvimpaga jeluvondeс╕Нi
n─Бr─Бyaс╣Зu с╕Нitaс╕Н─У vunnata v─Ус╣Еkaс╣нavibhuс╕Нu …. ─Бdi ..
The Adi-Purusha, Achyutha, the firm one, the limitless one, the sinless one
That Lord himself is Hari, this Lord of Venkata!
During the apocalypse, when the waters inundated
the entire universe, the Lord who was afloat, reclining upon
a tiny banyan leaf, as a baby,
that Lord of Sree is the Lord of Venkata!
To destroy the arrogance of king Bali, taking a form which reached
up to the sky, the Lord who measured the entire earth in one step,
and shook the entire universe with the powerful big toe,
that Paramatma is the Lord of Venkata!
In the milky ocean, with Sesha as the couch,
as Sree devi and Bhu devi press His feet lovingly,
with Brahma and others serving Him closely, the Lord who
rejoices thus, that Narayana Himself is this Supreme Lord of Venkata!

You are the God in everything! Befitting Goddess You have as Your consort!
In what manner can we praise you both?
Like a pair of the full moon and its light, like the flowers and their fragrance!
Attaining supremacy, She made Your bosom her abode!
A treasure of glorious wealth, the birth place of Madana
She has beautifully become Your royal abode!
Like the milky ocean and its purity, like the gold and its inherent glow!
She united herself with You, holding Your palm!
An embodiment of highest virtues, the supreme fortune of the worlds
She has abidingly become Your precious wealth!
The mother who created everyone, that Lakshmi who is the тАШAdimoolaтАЩ
Eagerly She adorned Your body as a sacred ornament!
In this manner, Sree Venkatesha, She-the supremely bewitching one,
As she joined You, Your prosperity dazzled in effulgence!

He is the boon bestowing Lord who resides on Venkatadri!
The gloriously manifested tall God!!
The one from whose every hair follicle burst forth the crores of Universes,
He is that splendidly resplendent gigantic Lord!
With the fourteen worlds that are within Him, and yet outside Him,
He is that great Lord who measured them with His feet!
Praising whose qualities, the Veda-Shastras never get exhausted,
He is that Primal Lord who is the repository of many great attributes!
To create and protect the multitude of demigods,
He is the Primal cause, the father of Manmatha!
Joyously wielding the Shanka-Chakra, the one who cuts asunder demons,
that many-formed Lord He is!
By placing Sree on His chest, becoming Sree Venkatesha
He is that eternal God who protects Sharanagathas!

talagakiс╣нu raс╣Еgamadhyapu toс╣нс╣нelan

cilup─Бla selavit┼Н ┼Ыr─лraс╣Еga ┼Ыi┼Ыuvu …. tolli ..
adivo kamalajuni tiruv─Бradhanaс╣Г banaga
adana kamalabhav─Бс╣Зс╕Нamanu toс╣нс╣нelun
udadhulu taraс╣Еgamulu n┼лcag─Б n┼лg─лni

v─Уdamule c─Уrulai velayaс╣Еga ┼Ы─Ус╣гuс╕Н─У
p─Бdukonu toс╣нс╣нelai paragag─Бnu
┼Ыr─лd─Уvit┼Н g┼лс╕Нi ┼Ыr─л v─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─У┼Ыuс╕Н─У

Since, at the very beginning, He was swinging in the banyan leaf cradle
So, with supreme authority, He is swinging, this baby of Srirangam!
On the waves of the beautiful damsel KaveriтАЩs encircling arms,
in the middle of the cradle like island,
as she sang beholding Him again and again, He is swinging
with milk drooling from the corner of His smiling lips, this baby of Srirangam!
Behold! As though Lord Brahma was performing the Tiruvaradhanam1,
in the cradle of the lotus like Universe,
when the waves of the ocean were swaying,
with undisturbed glory, is swinging this baby of Srirangam!
With the Vedas as the ropes of the cradle,
with Sesha spreading out firmly as the cradle,
Along with Sree-Devi, Sree Venkatesha Himself
is the one who is relaxing as the baby of Srirangam!!!
1 Tiruvaradhanam: The propitious daily worship.

bс╣Ыnd─Бrak─Бdh─л┼Ыavanditapad─Бbjaс╣Г …. vand─У ..

I worship Vasudeva!
That one who is revered by the head of all demigods!
The one like a black cloud, who from the confines of Lakshmi’s bosom
gets smeared by sandal paste, that one with an immaculate body
who is garlanded with Mandara flowers, who shines with a crown,
the father of Kandarpa1, the lotus navelled one!
The one whose chest is adorned by the glittering Kaustubha jewel,
the one who has the king of birds as His vehicle, the lotus eyed one
the one praised by the Vedas, the one who in His true form reclines on
Sesha - the king of serpents, and the one who is the refuge of all divinities!
The Lord of Karipura, the one who is always engaged in protection
the one who blessed the elephant king at the time of need, with His lotus like hands,
the one with Lotus eyes, the one who shines brilliantly with the discus,
On that Lord of Tiru Venkatachala, I meditate!
This Sankirtana is composed on Kanchi Varadaraja Perumal!

  1. Kandarpa : Manmatha

O mind! In your thought and also outwardly,
say тАШGovindaтАЩ, тАШGovindaтАЩ and pay reverence!
All deities are but HariтАЩs Incarnations

The feet which Lord Brahma washed with reverence,
they are the Supreme Brahman themselves!
The feet which Vasudha1 joyfully worshipped,
On king BaliтАЩs head this foot was placed,
Valiantly, this foot had measured the entire sky,
Indra was protected by the grace of these feet!
KaminiтАЩs2 sins were washed away by these feet
These are the feet that were placed on KaliyaтАЩs head
With love, Sree-sati massages these feet
These are the feet of the extraordinary horse (Lord Hayagreeva)
For the highest of sages in very many ways
these divine feet grant salvation!
Proving that тАШTiru VenkatagiriтАЩ is eternal,
the Parama-Padam3 is at your feet!
1.Vasudha is mother earth, the consort of Vishnu
2.The reference here is to Ahalya, whose sins were absolved by the touch of Lord
RamaтАЩs feet
3.The supreme realm

You are that, what one perceives you as
If appraised rightly, however the dough is, so turns out the pancake!
Vaishnavas serve You with love as тАШVishnuтАЩ
Vedantins call You the тАШPara BrahmanтАЩ
Shaivaites and some devotees say You are тАШShivaтАЩ
Kapalikas praise You as тАШAdi BhairavaтАЩ!
Shakteyas worship You as the тАШDivine SaktiтАЩ
Perceiving You in various ways, people worship You as their thoughts run
In affluence with pride, to those who take You as nothing, to them You are nothing
To the wise ones who take You as the superior most, You are the most magnificent!
In You there are no short comings, as the lotus rises just to the level of water
Around river Bhagirathi it is the same water that springs in the wells,
If You are Sree Venkatapathi, the Lord who accepts us,
right here I surrender unto You totally! For me this is the highest truth!

We beheld your presence, O Purushottama!
Do not let go of us, O Konetiraayaa!1
You ruled over us lovingly by your own wish, O family deity!
You are the real treasure our fore-fathers bestowed upon us after realizing!
You are the dark blue cloud who quenches our thirst in a loving manner!
You are Srinivasa, seated in our minds!
You are the Parijatha2 which we have gained by mere thought!
You are the Chintamani3 who protects us to our hearts’ content!
You are the Kamadhenu4 who blesses us and grants desired boons!
Being our only refuge, You protect us, O Dharanidhara5!
O life saving powerful incantation,
O disease destroying divine medication,
O inseparable soul тАУ relation,
You won over us, O Lord Sree Venkatanatha!!
1.Konetiraya means тАШThe Lord of the KoneruтАЩ. Koneru is the holy Pushkarini tank.
2.The Parijatha flower
3.The wish fulfilling gem
4.The wish yielding cow
5.The Lord who bore the earth

Overflowing with sweetness, in YashodaтАЩs courtyard, He is the Pearl,
The possessor of great glories, the child of Devaki!
For the Gopika women, He is the easily accessible Ruby
For Kamsa the obstinate, He is the tough Diamond
Illuminating the three worlds, He is a green Emerald
He is closely within us, this little Krishna!
When engaged in love making with Rukmini, He is the Coral of her red lips
While lifting the huge Govardhana hill, He is the yellow Sapphire
In between the Conch and the Discus, He shines eternally as the Vaidurya
Being our only means, He protects us, this Lotus eyed Lord!
On the hoods of Kaliya, He shone as the Pushyaraga
Ruling over Sree Venkatadri, He is the blue Sapphire
Residing in the milky ocean eternally, He is the divine gem
He moved about like a small boy, this Lotus naveled Lord!

Residing in the hills, He is the Konetiraaya !
He is the one who can bestow boons as huge as mountains!
To тАШKuruvaratti NambiтАЩ the potter,
He bestowed all that he asked for!
To the king тАШTondamaanтАЩ who was waging wars,
He appeared wherever he had promised!
To тАШAnantalvarтАЩ with utmost delight,
sharing his drudgery, He carried the sand weight!
With тАШTirumalanambiтАЩ, in the form of friendly gestures,
He joyfully shared some banter and gossips!
On тАШTirukachhinambiтАЩ who was in Kanchi,
He showered His grace and made him come to His place!
Lord Venkatesha cannot be measured by us,
with His bounteous compassion, the benevolent Lord graces us!!
1.Kuruvaratti Nambi was a potter by profession residing at Tirumala, and was the
great devotee of the Lord.
2.Tondaman was an emperor
3.Anantalvar was a disciple of Ramanujacharya, who was sent to Tirumala by the
Acharya to maintain a flower garden for Lord Venkateswara’s daily worship.
4.Tirumala Nambi was the maternal uncle of Ramanuja, who taught him the Ramayan
at Tirumala.
5.Tirukachhi Nambi (Kanchipurna) was a disciple of Yamunacharya, and it was he who
instructed Ramanuja according to the Lord’s wishes.

To Narayana, many salutations!
To the one who is praised by sage Narada, many salutations !
To the Vanquisher of Mura, the destroyer of mortal ills, Mukunda, Madhava!
to the one who moves mounted on Garuda, that lotus naveled one,
the Supreme being who releases us from earthly ties,

gaс╕Нi d─Бс╣нinapuс╕Нe kaivalyamu….n─Бn─Бс╣нi..

naginagi k─Бlamu n─Бс╣нakamu
yeguvane ┼Ыr─лv─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─У┼Ыvaru с╕Н─Уlika
gaganamu m─лdidi kaivalyamu….n─Бn─Бс╣нi..
The day to day existence is mere play,
The one which is perceived without being seen is salvation!
Birth is a truth, death is a truth,
in-between, our doings are but a play!
Right in front exists the world,
but the final destination is only salvation!
Food we consume, clothes we wear,
the deeds in-between are mere play!
The self acquired dual-karmas,
if we cross, only then is the salvation!
Binding are sins, inexhaustible are merits,
in-between, the passing time is but mere play!
High up is Sree Venkateshwara, the ruling deity,
there beyond the sky is the salvation!!

Praises and encomiums many, to the beautiful mother!
Praises to Her face as sweet as sugar!
Filled with all the graceful coquettery,
to those penetrating looks of Hers, many praises!
When taunting her Lord with languishing words,
to Her pretense of anger and tantrums, many praises!
When standing beside Her Lord, with a lute in her hand,
to the lustre of Her bounteous bosom, many praises!
When leaning on to Her majestic consort,
to Her slender waist, many praises!
To the one with a cross belt and pearl strings,
to that one with a bodily fragrance of sandal, many praises!
To those arms of Hers which surround Her consort
Lord Venkata with great delight, many praises!

He is Sesha! Sree Venkatadri Sesha!
The one who is equal to Garuda in every respect, that Sesha!
Manifested with a thousand hoods, this Sesha
With a resplendent body like that of dazzling diamonds, this Sesha

Constantly he provides the shade to Hari, this Sesha!

He has coiled into circles, this dazzling Sesha
With a thousand tongues is this Sesha
He is adept in praising Hari, this Sesha!
He always waits eagerly to perform duties, this Sesha
Worshipped first by all Gods is this Sesha
For Sree Venkatapathi and Alamelumanga,
he is the firm eternal couch, this Sesha!

In this manner, when You mounted Garuda,
the four directions broke apart!
When Garuda flew up, with a deafening sound
emitting bright flashes of light,
the Vedanta and the Veda,
the sky and the worlds, all trembled!
When You rode on Garuda at great speed,
with great rage,
all the worlds became subdued
and whirled in the four directions!
Onto the saddle of the golden Garuda of Yours,
when You mounted,
the groups of Rakshasas, startled in fear,
got inundated in Your divine glory, O Venkataramana!

You are the one to be proclaimed! You are the one, you are the one!
The representative of the Lord of Sree, O Sena Mudalari!
Standing right in front of Lord Hari,
You are the God who allows all other Gods to see Him!
In which ever manner perceived, for the Lord of Lakshmi,
you are the true servant, O Sena Mudalari!
As thousands of servants with golden batons serve you
sending orders in all directions, you are the courageous one!
You reign over the inhabitants of the three worlds
as your own children, O Sena Mudalari!
Crushing the ruling Asuras into smithereens in a valorous way,
you ruled over the entire universe as one kingdom!
O Lord of Sootravathi1, you are the great treasure of
Lord Venkatapathi, O Sena Mudalari!

Salutations to you, O divine Discus who destroys demons!
O victorious one in battle, O Discus of the great Lord!
O divine Discus with sixteen arms
Holding divine weapons, O strong Discus
O Discus who stands with three eyes
Do forgive me completely, O shining Discus!
O eternal Discus with the six angular corners
With thousands of sharp cutting edges, O divine Discus
O Discus emitting flames of eternal fires that reach upwards
With affection, do protect your devotees, O Discus!
O Discus with the effulgence of crores of suns and moons
O Discus worshipped even by demigods
O Discus resplendently wielded by the right hand of Sree Venkatesha
Here, do rule over us, who are the servants of yours, O Discus!!!

There! O there is Sri HariтАЩs abode!
It is but SeshaтАЩs ten thousand hoods!
That is Venkatachala, the superior most,
It is rare and precious to even Brahma and others,
It is the eternal abode of all sages,
Behold it! Salute it! It is filled with eternal bliss!
Right ahead is the Seshachala Mountain!
The true living abode of all heavenly deities,
Just a threshold away is the real treasure,
those golden cliffs, full of supreme bliss !
Bestower of eternal beatitude, there it is, the Lords city,
It is Sree VenkataтАЩs bounteous prosperity
If you can perceive it, it is your fortune in all its entirety,
and the purest of all purity!

How did You learn, O Lord, the skill of mounting so many Vahanas?
This is the reason O Hari, we appreciate You immensely!
You mounted onto Garuda on that day,
when You wanted to lift off the Parijatha tree!
With greatness, You mounted the chariot on that day,
when You blessed the Brahmin ladies with deliverance!
Beautifully, You mounted onto тАШPushpakaтАЩ, the flying chariot of Kubera,
to lovingly bring back Sita-devi!
Befittingly, You mounted onto Hanuman to wage a battle,
and to see the mighty array of the vanara forces!
At the end, You mounted onto the might horse
to counter Adharma and destroy it!
And upon Sree Venkatadri, You mounted the palanquin
along with Lakshmi, to proceed for Your wedding!!!

He, the Lord of all the worlds, receives gracefully,
in a pristine manner, the Pushpayagam1!
Along with various mantras, along with the Veda Goshas
with the recitation of Tiruvaimozi2, along with dancing damsels
along with praises sung by poets, along with pleasing worship,
He is adorned by the Pushpayagam!
Along with camphor arathi, along with pure sandal paste,
along with plentiful incense, along with the Tirumandikapu3
along with agreeable Paniyarams4, with duly offered abundant luxuries,
the Almighty receives the Pushpayagam!
Along with the umbrellas, with the fans, with beetle leaf offerings,
joyously receiving in this manner the various kinds of worship,
Behold! He excelled in brilliance, this Lord Sree Venkateshwara,
in the glorious Pushpayagam!
1.10th day of Brahmotsavam
2.Nammalwar’s work of one thousand Prabandhams
3.Waving of the lamp
4.Food offerings

panigonduru m─Бprapannulu
kaviyeс╕Нikannulu kamal─Бkс╣гunilayaс╣Г -
danuvu paratu raс╣нu hari s─Уvakulu …. marigi ..
palikeс╕Нipalukulu param─Бtmunikai
yalavaraturu ┼Ыaraс╣З─Бgatulu

talakolupudu r─Бtadiyyulu …. marigi ..

muriyucu j─Уturu mumukс╣гulu
yiravuga ┼Ыr─лv─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─У┼Ыvarumatam─У
sirula nammuduru ┼Ыr─лvaiс╣гс╣Зavulu …. marigi ..
They themselves are like our Gods!
Those great ones who praise Hari ardently!
The ears that can hear, they use them only to listen to
the glories of Vishnu, our Prapannas!
The eyes that can see, they fix them only upon
the Lotus eyed Lord, the servants of Hari!
The words they utter, they are accustomed to use them
only to praise Paramatma, the Sharanagathas!
The thoughts that they think of, they concentrate them upon
Lord Dharanidhara, these Tadeeyas1!
Their hands, they joyously offer in the service of
Sree-Pathi, these Mumukshus2!
They resolutely consider SreeVenkateshwaras doctrine
as the true treasure, these Sree Vaishnavas!
1.Tadeeyas are тАШThose who belong to HimтАЩ (i.e those who surrender to Lord Hari)
2.Those who aspire for Moksha, i.e Salvation

v─Уdan─Бr─Бyaс╣Зayaс╣Зс╣н─У v─лс╕Н─Ус╣нibandhamulu

O Lord, is there any shortcoming in You? Our thoughts alone are deficient!
Getting caught in thousands of Karmas, we become vexed!
Though by saying тАШHariтАЩ even once, all accrued sins get destroyed,
yet strong faith never originates in us!
By saying тАШNarasimhaтАЩ we acquire various merits
how can we ever repay for it?
By saying тАШDeva! Jagannatha!тАЩ will not the cycle of births be severed!
But my mind is never under my own control!
By saying тАШGovinda!тАЩ though there are no posts that cannot be attained,
yet we while away our time aimlessly!
тАШVeda-Narayana!тАЩ if we say, our attachments will let go
Is there anything greater than this in the three worlds, from ever before?
O consort of Sree Devi! O Sree Venkatesha!
You alone save us in every way!

─Бkaс╣нiv─Бniki nannam─У brahmamu

kai koni karmiki k─Бlam─У brahmamu
┼Ыr─лk─Бntunipai jiс╣Г tadi y─Уl─Б …. paс╣нс╣нina ..
bhuvi saс╣Гs─Бriki putrule brahmamu

bhava matanikс╣Ыp─У brahmamu …. paс╣нс╣нina ..
All that which is acquired is the Supreme,
for the highly ignorant one. Why at all a God for him?
For a lowly beggar, gold is the Supreme
The body is Supreme for one who is aroused
For a lustful one, women are the Supreme
The inner effulgent eternal truth, why for them?
For a hungry one, food is the Supreme
The world is Supreme for one who is enamored by it
For a diligent worker, time itself is Supreme
Why for them, the thought upon the Lord of Sree!
For an earthly Samsarin, progeny is the Supreme
For these people, this alone is the ever-fresh way of life!
Whereas, for the dasas of Sree Venkatesha,
in worldly existence, His grace alone is the Supreme!

paramavaiс╣гс╣Зavula bh─Бgyaс╣Г bidiv┼Н
nirativ─Бralake n─У mokkedanu …. parama ..
talaca rokappuс╕Нu dharaс╣Зi bh┼Нgamulu
talaca ritaramatadaivamula
talatu rokaс╣нi harid─Бsulad─Бsyamu
talapu m┼Нkс╣гamulatagulami (me?) g─Бna …. parama ..

k┼Нruduru tadiyyak┼Нс╣нlasaс╣Еgamu

This is the fortune of Parama-Vaishnavas!
Constantly I pay my salutations to them!
They donтАЩt think even once of earthly comforts,
they donтАЩt think of the Gods of other philosophies!
But they think of being the servants of the servants of Hari,
because their thoughts are towards Moksha!
They donтАЩt desire for posts like that of Brahma and others,
they do not even desire the pleasure of the highest kind!
But they desire the company of crores of Tadeeyas1,
because their desires are coupled with Bhakti!
They do not accept Karmas, not even merits,
they do not accept arrogance even once!
Offering their hearts in surrender to the Supreme Venkatesha,
they have already attained the highest post!

  1. Those who have surrendered to the Lord

You are my property, and I am Your property!
For this reason, why donтАЩt You stay in my house for ever?
O Hari! My Acharya bestowed Your perceivable form
unto me long ago, with abounding joy!
O Nara-Hari! I did not know You by any unjust means
Is it right then for You to go away even by mistake?
Your consort Lakshmi is my mother, You are my father
You alone are my physical existence and soul-relation!
However great a sinner I am,
can You ever let go of me intentionally?
The many Vedas conferred on You the appropriate title of
тАШBhakta VatsalaтАЩ1, and proclaimed the same on this earth!
Now, O Sree Venkatesha, remembering that,
do come to me in a befitting way!
This is the song that Annamacharya sang to his personal deity!

  1. Bhakta Vatsala - The one who is affectionately graceful to His devotees.

Recite this and live, all of you, O people!
Dwell upon it, this is the Narayana Astakshari!
Having obtained it, this is the one that was recited by Shuka previously
This is the one that was recited by Veda-Vyasa
This is the one that was recited by the Vaishnavas during the ancient times
This is the adorable Narayana Astakshari!
This is the one eternally studied by the sages
This is the one recited by Lord Brahma to win over troubles
This is the one ardently recited by Prahalada
This is the only means, the Narayana Astakshari!
This is the one that is recited by the Devas diligently
This is the one recited by the Brahmin clan
Time and again, becoming Sree Venkateshwaras name
it exists on this earth, this Narayana Astakshari!

O people, today is Narasimha Jayanthi!
Bringing happiness to all divinities, it bestowed propitious-ness!
On Vaishaka Suddha Chaturdashi, a Saturday,
during the twilight hours, the Lord of Ahobilam
emerged magnificently from the pillar
and on the threshold, ripped apart Hiranyakasipu with His nails!
The one in the form of a man-beast, with many hands
holding the Shanka-Chakra and other weapons,
He stood after having rescued and blessed Prahalada
inside the great тАШBrahmandaтАЩ1 like cave!
Upon a golden throne, in the royal court,
placing Lakshmi on his thigh, He exists!
Behold! Upon Sree Venkatagiri, as the Adi-Purusha
He unfailingly bestows great boons!

All your secretive desires, do enjoy to the fullest!
To Your reigning Queen, and to You, Pallandu! Pallandu!
With shining thighs and arms adorned by emerald studded ornaments,
leaning onto Her companion, the mother of the one who wields
the green bow2, sprinkles from her golden like cupped palms,
the green camphor upon You! Pallandu! Pallandu!
With Her sweet secret words, in privy, she made You faint in ecstasy
with the glow radiating from Her tender nails,
when Her companions offered the water lilies to Her hands,
She showered them upon You intentionally! Pallandu! Pallandu!
In the magnificent mansion, Alamelumanga,
in order to pacify Your anger, gratifies You with Her Love
and unites with You in an embrace, O Venkatesha!
Many times over, for the two of You, Pallandu! Pallandu!

Do what You want with me! It is up to You!
My guru made me hold You feet, I will not let go!
Thinking тАЬhe chants my name at all times,
what may he ask of me?тАЭ, do not get worried.
Earlier itself, my Acharya blessed me with everything
today when questioned тАШWhy this?тАЩ, I will never let go of his principles!
тАЬWith love he worships me, placing me in his house,
what might be the reason?тАЭ- do not think in this manner.
My devout Acharya is the very reason between You and me!
If asked тАШwhy this love?тАЩ, my Acharya offered me unto You!
тАЬRepeatedly why he worships me?тАЭ
do not get vexed in this manner, O Sree Venkatesha!
Joyously my Acharya did the same thing,
this remains for eternity, You and I will never be separated!

yivvala vic─Бri├▒cav─У iс╣Гdir─Бramaс╣З─Б …. evvaru ..
veс╣Зс╣нabeс╣нс╣нi k─Бmakr┼Нdhavitatulu cuс╣нс╣нi nannu
toс╣Зс╣нi m─л s─Уvaku nannu d┼лramu s─Уse
kaс╣Зс╣нakapuс╣нindriy─Бlu kaс╕Нuhita┼Ыatrulai

Who is the refuge for me? Where is the right knowledge?
Do think about it, O Indira-Ramana!
Not letting go, the overpowering Kama and Krodha have surrounded me,
and have refrained me from performing service unto You!
The troublesome senses, becoming the foes to my well being,
have not allowed me to take the path to the attainable Moksha!
Over and over again, my desires have prevented me from enjoying
blissfully the Sree-Vaishnava dharma, causing me immense distress!
This attractive Samsara has obstructed me from
gaining the merits of the superior service of Acharya!
This body full of malice has obstructed the mind from mellowing,
and has made way for ignorance by deceiving me!
Here, O Sree Venkatesha, as You rule over me,
eternally Your grace alone has made me pure and pristine!

If not for You, how under the influence of the rigid minded Sunyavadins1,
could the wise people rise above and survive!
In the past, the worlds were filled with
the doctrine of тАШNirakaraтАЩ2!
Proving that it is untrue, by showing Your form of Trivikrama,
You established the authority of the Vedas!
Hearing the words of those who proclaim тАШAham BrahmasmiтАЩ3,
all devotion had been blown away into the winds!
During that time itself, You showed to Prahalada, in front of Hiranyakasipu,
the difference between the тАШRulerтАЩ and the тАШServantтАЩ!
Because of the unrighteous injunctions that proclaim тАШEverything is oneтАЩ
all merit was lost and people became lowly!
Then, saying тАЬI am the HighestтАЭ, O Sree Venkatesha,
You manifested Yourself and prospered as the wonder on the mountain!
1.The Buddhists
2.The doctrine of the formless God, the Nirguna Brahman
3.The doctrine which holds that the Jiva itself is the Lord (Advaita)

Alas! Those who argue perversely never feel ashamed!
How did this wicked doctrine of demons come to exist?
They donтАЩt accept to wear Your mudras, they donтАЩt accept to be Your servants,
the desirable devotion for You, they donтАЩt accept at all!
They donтАЩt accept the chanting of Your name, they call You as a nameless one
Yet they argue that they are Vaishnavas!
Even during the Pitru-Karmas, they donтАЩt accept Your prasadam,
they refuse to wear the Urdhva-pundaras as though it is harmful!
They worship You alongside the other inferior Gods
Yet they think that they are Vaishnavas!
When they come across Sree Vaishnavas, they donтАЩt greet them with
folded hands, and they feel that they have seen their enemies!
Also they say that Vaikunta is impermanent
Yet they say тАЬAre we not VaishnavasтАЭ!
Like Ravana and others they perform Yagnas
and they also study the Vedas!
Eternally O Sree Venkatesha! Without knowing Your glories
they proclaim themselves as Vaishnavas and pretend to be so!
Having studied extensively the inner truths of the Srutis and Smritis, Ramanuja laid down the
rules for prapannas. One of the basic duties of a true Vaishnava is to undergo the Pancha -
Samskara rituals. This involves the wearing of the Mudras, that is the permanent marks of
Shanka-Chakra, and also applying regularly the marks of the Tiruman - Sree Choornam at the
twelve appropriate places on the body. Sree Vedanta Desika quotes the authority for the wearing
of the Mudras in his work Saccharitra-raksha.
рдкреНрд░ рддреЗ рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдгреЛрд░рдмреНрдЬрдЪрдХреНрд░реЗ рдкрд╡рд┐рддреНрд░реЗ рдЬрдиреНрдорд╛рдореНрднреЛрдзрд┐рдВ рддрд░реНрддрд╡реЗ рдЪрд░реНрд╖рдгреАрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╛-ред
рдореВрд▓реЗ рдмрд╛рд╣реНрд╡реЛрд░реНрджрдзрддреЗрд╜рдиреНрдп рдкреБрд░рд╛рдг рд▓рд┐рдЩреНрдЧрд╛рдиреНрдпрдЩреНрдЧреЗ рддрд╛рд╡рдХрд╛рдиреНрдпрд░реНрдкрдпрдиреНрддрд┐рее
The best among men wear the pure insignia of Vishnu’s lotus and discus on their arms to cross
the ocean of Samsara. Some wear those insignia on the body.
рдПрднрд┐рд░реНрд╡рдпрдореБрд░реВрдХреНрд░рдорд╕реНрдп рдЪрд┐рд╣реНрдиреИ рд░рдЩреНрдХрд┐рддрд╛ рд▓реЛрдХреЗ рд╕реБрднрдЧрд╛ рднрд╡рд╛рдо-ред
рддрджреНрд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдгреЛ- рдкрд░рдордВ рдкрджрдВ рдпреЗрд╜рдзрд┐рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрдиреНрддрд┐ рд▓рд╛рдЮреНрдЫрд┐рддрд╛-рее
Like those who go to the abode of Vishnu, being marked by the insignia of the discs and conch,
we too shall be impressed by the emblems of Vishnu and gain affluence here and hereafter.
рдЙрдкрд╡реАрддрд╛рджрд┐рд╡рдвреНрдврдВрд░реНрдпрд╛- рд╢рдЩреНрдХрдЪрдХреНрд░рд╛рджрдпрд╕реНрддрдерд╛ред
рдмреНрд░рд╛рд╣реНрдордгрд╕реНрдп рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖реЗрдг рд╡реИрд╖реНрдгрд╡рд╕реНрдп рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рдд-рее
The Brahmanas, particularly the Vaishnavas, should wear the marks of the conch and
discus as they wear the sacred thread.
рд╣рд░реЗ- рдкрджрд╛рдХреГрддрд┐рдВ рдЖрддреНрдордиреЛ рд╣рд┐рддрд╛рдп рдордзреНрдпреЗ рдЪреНрдЫрд┐рджреНрд░рдореВрдШреНрд╡рдкреБрдгреНрдбреНрд░рдореН
рдпреЛ рдзрд╛рд░рдпрддрд┐ рд╕ рдкрд░рд╕реНрдп рдкреНрд░рд┐рдпреЛ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рд╕ рдкреБрдгреНрдпрд╡рд╛рдиреН рднрд╡рддрд┐ рд╕ рдореБрдХреНрддрд┐рдорд╛рдиреН рднрд╡рддрд┐рее
He who for the good of himself, wears the Urdhva-pundra resembling the footprints of Hari,
becomes the favourite of the Paramatman, virtous and liberated.
Some of the other rules for Prapannas as laid down by Ramanuja are
(1) Never consider Lord Sriman Narayana as just one among the host of other deities. He is the
overlord of all, the sole ruler of the entire universe. He is the one who has no equal.
(2) True devotees of Vishnu are as respectable as the Lord Himself. Only by worshipping the
holy feet of Sree Vaishnavas, one can attain Him easily.
(3) Always have a desire to partake Tirta-Prasadam.
(4) Chant the Dvayam constantly.
True Sree Vaishnavas are those who follow whole heartedly the injunctions of the scriptures and
the commandments of Acharya Ramanuja. They never hesitate to wear the mudras or the
Tiruman-Sree Choornams. Only such people who innately follow the Vaishnava code of
conduct are true Sree Vaishnavas.

This is the famed Putrotsavam1 on this earth!
Today is Krishna Jayanthi, O folks!
The one who has the entire Brahmanda within His stomach,
amazingly He was borne by Devaki in her womb!
The one who could not be perceived by the Devathas even upon searching,
here, how could Vasudeva see Him, O folks!
The Highest of the highest Lord Purushottama, today
has amazingly become a baby in a cradle, O folks!
The one who partakes all the Yagna-offerings eternally,
as a baby son, He is suckling on the breasts of His mother, O folks!
Being the son-in-law of the milky ocean and never being separated from it,
here, how is it that the festival of breaking the milk pots hung high up
has become his passion!
Being used to sporting upon the Sree Venkatadri hill,
His baby like prattles are ever increasing, O folks!

bhaktasulabhuс╕Нanu paratantruс╕Нu hari
yuktis─Бdhya mide yokarik─л g─Бс╕Нu …. bhakta ..
ninupagul┼Нkamula niс╣Зс╕Нinaviс╣гс╣Зuс╕Нu
manujuс╕Нa n─Бl┼Н manikiyayye

poс╕Нavaku boс╕Нavagupuruс╣г┼Нttamu с╕Нide

The one affable to devotees, the one under the control of devotees, Hari!
He is attainable with resolve, He does not belong to anyone!
Vishnu who is pervading the wholesome worlds,
He exists within me who am a mere human!
That mantra which is proclaimed by the Vedas,
Has become established permanently on the tip of the tongue!
The Lord who ruled over the demigods,
He ruled over me who am a lowly one in all respects!
The powerful consort of Lakshmi, Sree Hari,
here, He himself stands in our house!
The higher than the highest Purushottama,
accepted the trivial worship offered by our hands!
Not letting go of us, and remaining ever inseparable,
He is there with us, this Sree Venkateshwara!

ekkaс╕Нi narakamulu yekkaс╕Нi mс╣Ыtyuvu m─Бku

Where is hell? Where is death for us?
We have drunk in abundance the nectar of Your name!
Eagerly, O Sree-pathi, when we associated with Your dasas,
the fear of YamaтАЩs attendants got suppressed!
Joyously, the moment we wore the impressions of Your Shanka-Chakra,
all the punishments of eternal time were destroyed!
The moment we took the path leading to Your glorious city,
the fierce тАШSouthern PathтАЩ leading to hell ended!
When we resided at Your Tirupathi just for a night,
the wounds caused by the hells of Kala-Sutra got healed!
The moment we chose to chant Your divine mantras,
the accounts of Chitragupta got annulled!
O Sree Venkateshwara, the moment we surrendered unto You,
the holy Vaikuntam came onto our palms!

erugudu rindaru neс╣Яig─лneс╣Яagaru
hari d─Бn─У nijaparam─Бtumani …. erugudu ..
nalin─Бsanu с╕Нeс╣Яugu n─Бradu с╕Нeс╣Яugu
koladi ┼Ыivu с╕Нeс╣Яugu guhu с╕Нeс╣Яugu

talapa viс╣гс╣Зuс╕Н─У paratatvamani …. erugudu ..
berasi prahl─Бduс╕Нu bh─лс╣гmuс╕Нu janakuс╕Нu

varusa neс╣Яuguduru vaс╕Нi rahasyamuga
hari yitaс╕Н─У param─Бtmuс╕Нani …. erugudu ..
teliyadagina didi teliyar─Бni didi

kalavella delipe v─Ус╣Еkaс╣нar─Бyaс╕Нu …. erugudu ..
All these will know! Though knowing, yet they will not know,
that Hari alone is the true Paramatma!
Brahma who sits in the lotus knows, Narada knows,
His capacity Lord Shiva knows, Guha1 knows,
here, Kapila knows, Manu knows!
All these know in their thought that Vishnu alone is the Paratattva!
Having attained Him, Prahalada, Beeshma, King Janaka,
King Bali, Shuka, and Kaala2,
all these people know the secret that He,
Lord Hari alone is the Paramatma!
This is the one to be known, this is the one that cannot be known!
Even after knowing it, this cannot be known!
Here, these great ones realized that this is the Supreme,
and all of that is made known by Lord Venkataraya!
1.Lord Subramanya
2.Lord Yama

inni l─Бgulac─Уtu liviyap┼Н kaс╕Нu
nennika kekkinac─Уtu liviyap┼Н …. inni ..

In these various ways are these hands!
Eternally glorious are these hands!
When He was sulking and pleading to be carried,
these were the hands that reached onto the mother!
When He was furious, these were the iron like hands
that uprooted the Govardhana mountain!
These are the tiny hands that squeezed and
firmly gripped the breast of Putana!
These are the hands that tended the cattle,
and threw the sands of Yamuna on Shepherd lasses!
He being the supreme consciousness, for all living beings,
these are the hands that bestowed boons!
These are the hands which point out the abode of salvation,
in the form of the Lord of Tiru Venkatagiri!

рдПрдорд┐рдиреЖрд▒рдЧрдирд┐рдордореНрдореБ рдиреЖрдХреНрдХреБрд╡рд╕реЗрд╕рд┐

─Тmineс╣Яaganimammu Nekkuvas─Уsi
рдПрдорд┐рдиреЖрд▒рдЧрдирд┐рдордореНрдореБ рдиреЖрдХреНрдХреБрд╡рд╕реЗрд╕рд┐

рдкрдЩреНрдХрдореЖрд▓реНрд▓ рдмреЛрдЧрдбрд┐рдЧреЖ рднрд╛рд╖реНрдпрдХрд╛рд░реБрд▓реБ реерее рдПрдореА рее
─Уmineс╣Яaganimammu nekkuvas─Уsi
p─Бmarula doс╕Нс╕Нaj─Уse bh─Бс╣гyak─Бrulu …. ─Уm─л ..
gatacanna v─Уd─Бlu kamalajunaku nicci
atanikaruс╣Зac─Уta nanniyu gani
gatil─Уkap┼Нyina kaliyugamuna vacci
pratip─Бli├▒cagalige bh─Бс╣гyak─Бrulu …. ─Уm─л ..
l┼Нkamella vellib┼Нg─Б l┼Нnan─У surala g─Бci
─Бkum─лda d─Уlinayatanikс╣Ыpa
k─Бkarimatamulella g─Бlibucci para miс╣нс╣н─У
paikonaga garuс╣Зi├▒ce bh─Бс╣гyak─Бrulu …. ─Уm─л ..
paс╣Еkajapuj─Уyi c─Бci p─Бdapubaramiccina -
v─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─У┼Ыukс╣Ыpat┼Нс╕Нa velaya d─Бn─У
teс╣Еkin─У voс╕Нayavarai tirumantradvay─Бna
paс╣Еkamella b┼Нgaс╕Нige bh─Бс╣гyak─Бrulu …. ─Уm─л ..
We who did not know anything, he elevated us!
He turned the ignorant ones into great ones, Bhasyakara!
The Lord who restored the Vedas to Brahma,
comprehending everything by the grace of that Lord,
and appearing in the forlorn Kali-yuga,
he bestowed protection, Bhasyakara!
The Lord who protected the Gods when the worlds were inundated in water,
by the grace of that Lord who floated on the banyan leaf,
throwing away all other worthless doctrines to the winds,
he blessed us to attain the Supreme easily, Bhasyakara!
The Lord who, with His lotus hands, showed that the Supreme is at His feet,
by the grace of that Lord Venkatesha,
as Udayavar, he became the strong foundation, and with the
Tirumantra and Dvayam he cleansed all sins, Bhasyakara!

Purport:

By the grace of the Supreme Lord Narayana who restored the Vedas to Barahma
in the form of Hayagriva, by the blessings of that true knower of the Vedas,
Sree Bhasyakara comprehended the true meanings of the Vedanta and
manifested himself on the earth to protect the people of Kail Yuga. By the grace
of Lord Venkateshwara who shows that Moksha can be attained only by
serving Him, Udayavar stood as the strong foundation of the SreeVaishnava
Siddantha and proved that all other worthless doctrines are fallacious and
impermanent.He established the true meanings of the Vedanta in his works.
With the Tirumantra and the Dvayam, he cleansed the sins of all beings and
showed the easy path to Parama Padam.
This Sankirtana has been composed on Sree Ramanujacharya.

Gatulanni Khilamaina

gatulanni khilamaina kaliyuga mandunu
gati y─лtaс╕Н─У c┼лpe ghana gurudaivamu …. gatu ..
y─лtani karuс╣Зan─Уk─Б yila vaiс╣гс╣Зavula maiti -
m─лtanivallan─У kaс╣Зс╣нi m─лtirumaс╣Зi
y─лtaс╕Н─Уk─Б vupad─У┼Ыa micce naс╣гс╣н─Бkс╣гari mantra-
m─лtaс╕Н─У r─Бm─Бnujulu yihaparadaivamu …. gatu ..
velayi├▒ce n─лtaс╕Н─Уk─Б v─Уdapu rahasyamulu
calimi n─лtaс╕Н─У c┼лpe ┼Ыaraс╣З─Бgati
nilipin─Б ─лtaс╕Н─Уk─Б nijamudradh─Бraс╣Зamu
malasi r─Бm─Бnujul─У m─Бс╣нal─Бс╕Н─У daivamu …. gatu ..
niyamamu l─лta с╕Н─Уk─Б nilipe brapannulaku
dayat┼Н m┼Нkс╣гamu c┼лpe daga n─лtaс╕Н─У
nayamai ┼Ыr─л v─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─У┼Ыunaga mekk─У v─Бkiс╣нanu
damaj┼лc─л mammu niс╣нс╣н─У talli taс╣Зс╕Нri daivamu …. gatu ..
In the evil ways of Kaliyuga,
he showed тАШThe pathтАЩ, the great divine guru!
IsnтАЩt it out of his compassion, here we are Vaishnavas,
Because of him, we could find the Tiruman1,
It is he who initiated us into the Ashtakshari mantra
He is Ramanuja, the God of here and hereafter!2
IsnтАЩt he the one who revealed the Vedic secrets
With benevolence he showed the path of Sharanagati
IsnтАЩt he the one who established the real Mudhra dharana3
In total, Ramanuja is a тАШSpeaking GodтАЩ!
IsnтАЩt he the one who laid the rules for Prapannas4
With compassion, he is the one who showed us Moksha.
Having beneficially climbed Lord Sree VenkateshaтАЩs hill,
he blesses us at the doorway5, as mother, father and God!
1.Sacred mud worn on the forehead as Naamam
2.When Ramanuja visited Tirumala, the Lord bestowed upon him both the
kingdoms- the spiritual as well as the material. Thus he is called as
тАШUbhaya Vibhuti PatiтАЩ or тАШThe God of here and hereafterтАЩ!
3.The method of Samashrayanam or Panchasamskara
4.Prapannas are those who have performed Sharanagathi
5.The Ramanuja shrine is at the doorway of the Tirumala temple

unnat┼Нnnatuс╕Нu vuс╕Нayavaru
yenna nanantuс╕Н─У y─л yuс╕Нayavaru …. unna ..
sarval┼Нkamula ┼Ы─Бstra rahasyamu
lurvi boс╕Нaye n─л yuс╕Нayavaru
p┼лrvapu v─Уd─Бnta puс╣Зya ┼Ыastramulu
nirvahi├▒ce nanniс╣н─Б nuс╕Нayavaru …. unna ..
vekkasapu ┼Ыr─л viс╣гс╣Зubhaktiy─У
vokkar┼лpam─У vuс╕Нayavaru
cakkanaina suj├▒─Бnamuna kiravai
vukku m─лс╣Яe nide vuс╕Нayavaru …. unna ..
kadise m┼Нkс╣гas─Бk─Бramu d─Бnai
vuduс╣нuna nilice n─л yuс╕Нayavaru
yidig┼Н ┼Ыr─л v─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─У┼Ыvaru y─лс╕Нai
podalucu nunn─Бс╕Нu bhuvi nuс╕Нayavaru …. unna ..
Higher than the highest is Udayavar1!
If understood rightly, he is limitless, this Udayavar!
The secrets of the scriptures of all the worlds,
he spread upon this earth, this Udayavar!
The ancient propitious scriptures of Vedanta,
he carried out in every way, Udayavar!
Of the supreme Vishnu Bhakti,
he is the sole personification, Udayavar!
Being the abode of benevolent тАШright-knowledgeтАЩ
he attained supremacy, Udayavar!
He himself being the very manifestation of Moksha,
he stood firmly, this Udayavar!
Behold! Being on par with Sree Venkateshwara,
on this earth, he prospers in all glory, Udayavar!
9495
1.Udayavar literally means тАШThe one who has been bestowedтАЩ. The Lord
Himself bestowed the two worlds, the material and the spiritual, unto
Ramanuja. Thus he is called Udayavar.

Sulabham─Б Manujulaku Haribhakti

sulabham─Б manujulaku haribhakti
valanondi marikad─Б vaiс╣гс╣Зavuс╕Нauс╣нa …. sulabham─Б ..
kodal─Уnitapamulu k┼Нс╣н─Бnag┼Нс╣нulu
nadana n─Бcari├▒ci yaс╣нam─лda
padilamaina karmabandhamu lanniyu
vadali├▒cukonikad─Б vaiс╣гс╣Зavuс╕Нauс╣нa …. sulabham─Б ..
taniv┼Нniy─Бgatantramulu lakс╣гalasaс╣Еkhya
anaghuс╕Нai c─Уsinayaс╣нam─лda
jananamulanniс╣нa janiyi├▒ci paramap─Б -
vanuс╕Нai marikad─Б vaiс╣гс╣Зavuс╕Нauс╣нa …. sulabham─Б ..
tirigitirigi pekkut─лrthamulanniyu -
naral─Уka s─Уvi├▒cinaс╣нam─лda
tiruv─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─Бcal─Бdhipuс╕Нaina karir─Бja -
varadunikс╣Ыpagad─Б vaiс╣гс╣Зavuс╕Нauс╣нa …. sulabham─Б ..
Is this easy for humans, devotion to Hari?
only upon lovingly desiring it, one can become a Vaishnava!
Only after performing crores and crores
of endless penances,
and only after getting freed from the strong
bondages of Karmas, one can become a Vaishnava!
Only after performing lakhs and lakhs of unending
Yagnas and rituals, as a pure hearted one,
only after taking births repeatedly and
becoming sanctified, one can become a Vaishnava!
Only after going on pilgrimages to various sacred teerthas,
and offering whole hearted worship,
only after begetting the grace of the Lord of TiruVenkatachala,
the savior of the elephant king, one can become a Vaishnava!

─Уdaivamu┼Ыr─лp─Бdanna (na?)khamuna buс╣нс╣нinagaс╣Еga
tril┼Нkap─Бvanamu c─Уyanu tripathag─Бmini ─Бyanu
y─Уdaivamun─Бbhinalinambuna janiyi├▒cinaajuс╣Зс╕Нu
akhil─Бс╣Зс╕Нambulu sс╣Ыjiyimpa nadhipati ─Бyanu

┼Ыr─лn─Бr─Бyaс╣Зad─Уvuс╣Зс╕Нani nammiyuс╣Зс╕Нuduru
─Бd─Уvuс╕Н─У sirula kanantavaraduс╕Нu tiruv─Ус╣Еkaс╣нa -
girin─Бthu с╕Нubhayavibh┼лtin─Бthuс╕Н─У n─Бn─Бthuс╕Нu .. ─Уdaivamu
Which Lords sacred toe-nail did Ganga take birth from,
and become divided into three, to sanctify the three worlds?
Which Lords lotus like navel did Brahma originate from,
to create the Universe and become the ruler?
Which Lords majestic chest did Lakshmi make Her abode,
and become the mother of this entire creation?
Which Lords glances bestow eternal bliss to
Indra and the host of other divinities?
Who is the Lord whom the Devas believe as the indweller
in all bodies, in the form of Lord Sree-Narayana?
That Lord alone, who is the eternal benefactor of wealth, the Lord of
Tiru Venkata, the Lord of the Ubhaya-Vibhutis, He alone is my Lord!!!

I meditate upon the child Gopala, who is constantly worshipped by the mind,
on that Lord who is fit to be contemplated upon at all times!
The one who shines brilliantly with a waist belt which is
decorated with precious gems and jingling bells that
sound musically as He toddles in a crooked way,
on Him who is an adept dancer, the splendidly graceful one, I meditate!
Having played with butter, the one whose hands have become smeared with it,
the one who shines in the thoughts of great divinities like Brahma and others,
that matchless Hari, who resides eternally on TiruVenkatachala,
on that Parama Purusha, Gopala-bala, I meditate!

Showing that the form of Vatapatrasayi is like this,
You have manifested in this reclining form, Govindaraja!
Lovingly extending Your feet towards the two Goddesses,
sleeping onto one side in a royal posture,
from the endless lotus in Your navel, You had borne
Brahma as Your son, Govindaraja!
Reclining on Sesha with wealth and prosperity,
bestowing grace on Your daasas,
and pouring venom of snakes onto
evil Rakshasas, O Govindaraja!
Wielding the Shanka-Chakra, with one arm extended over the leg,
and the other arm placed under the head,
reclining in Tirupathi, below Sree Venkatadri,
unhesitantly He bestows boons, Govindaraja!

Prostrations and salutations to the leader of the Raghu race,
the one who is revered by the residents of the divine worlds!
Prostrations and salutations to the one who is praised by Lord Shiva and Parvathi!
To the one who is the protector of true Dharma, the brave DasharathaтАЩs Rama,
the one who killed Tataka who resides in the skies,
the one who removed the curse of Ahalya, the one who destroyed the demon race,
the one who protected Vishwamitra from obstacles with much ease!
To the one who destroyed ShivaтАЩs bow, the sole Lord of SitaтАЩs body,
the enemy of Kara and Dushana, the one who destroyed the arrogance of Vali,
the one who protected Sugreeva and the others,
the one who built the bridge on the ocean, the one who is eternally with Lakshmana!
To the one who cut off the head of the illustrious Ravana, who blessed Vibheeshana,
the resident of Saketa pura (Ayodhya), that Raghava,
the matchless one, the one who resides on Sree Venkata,
the one who resides in the true abode of His own, the lotus eyed Lord!
Many salutations and prostrations!

Vishnu alone is the universal indweller!
The philosophy of Vaishnavism is everything!
The creation of the cosmic egg performed by Brahma,
The power of destruction possessed by Lord Shiva,
The efficiency of Indras rulership,
If rightly appraised, they are but Sree HariтАЩs glory!
The qualities present in the (panchabhutas) five elements
The movements of the (navagrahas) nine planets
The duties of the (trikalas) three time durations
All these are NarayanaтАЩs beautiful glories!
The ever present effects of Maya,
The bliss experienced at Parama Padam
All that which is extraordinarily reputed, all that which exists,
and everything, is but Sree VenkateshaтАЩs glory!

You view everyone with an equal eye, You are the God of Gods!
Then, why do you see my faulty traits?
Whether on flowers, whether on thorns
when the moon shines, will any harm befall the light?
Just like You save the pious, upon me who is a heap of sins
if you show mercy, will any harm befall Your grace?
The breeze that blows upon a cow, and likewise upon a dog
for the pure breeze, will there be any sin?
You who protects the Devas, to me who is the lowest of beings
if You show the way and protect, will it be a fault?
Entering the house of a тАШhigh casteтАЩ, and also that of a тАШlow catseтАЩ
will the sunlight in any way become inferior?
O granter of boons, SreeVenkatesha, residing within me
bestowing Your grace, will You not rescue me today??

Equating You and me, isnтАЩt it a crime!
The sun light which has spread out, can it become the sun itself?
The fish that is inside the ocean, can it become the ocean itself?
Is it not a creature that depends on the water!
Me who is within You, can I ever become You?
A mere puppet with Your support, am I not!
The slave of the King, will he become the king himself?
IsnтАЩt his post one that is created by the King!
Worshipping You naturally, how can I ever become You?
Serving You in an orderly manner, thus I live!
The water in the oyster, will it remain in its former state?
Will it not grow into a pearl and shine!
(So too) Constantly SreeVenkatesha, since we are Your Sharanagathas
we do not belong to any other world, we are but Muktas!!
The purport is:
By considering the Jivatman to be equal to the Lord, nothing can be
achieved. Rather it is a sin to think of oneself as equal to the Lord. Only
by duly Surrendering ourselves unto the Supreme Lord we can attain
the Highest!

Move away O commoners! Do not obstruct us!
This is our rich companionship. (Between me and the Lord)
The tongue that is soaked in the praises of Nara-Hari
it will not agree to praise others!
The head that has bowed down to the feet of Mura-Hara
it will not bow down to revere others!
The hands that have worshipped the Lord of Sree,
they will not extend forward to beg others!
The feet that have eagerly paced towards Hari,
they will not proceed to the house of sinners!
The mind that thinks of SreeVenkatapathi
it will not think of any other with any eagerness!
The body that is under the control of the Lord,
will not be under the control of anyone else!!

Understanding that Vishnu is everything is the right knowledge
Being a Vaishnava and serving Acharya, is the right knowledge!
The mountain like anger within oneself, when it is aroused
to gain control quickly and remain unmoved, is the right knowledge!
When strong desires arise for women other than ones own
not coming under its sway, is the right knowledge!
When one tries to lure into the pleasures of тАШhousesтАЩ and тАШluxuriesтАЩ
not falling prey to it, is the right knowledge!
The miseries arising out of binding relationships with relatives,
not getting dragged into them, is the right knowledge!
тАШWhatever happens is God ordainedтАЩ, thinking thus
and not finding fault with others, is the right knowledge!
At all times, SreeVenkateshwara who resides in our hearts
to behold his image, is the right knowledge!

iс╣Гtakaс╣Зс╣нe n─У munnadi yenta dalap┼Нsin─Бnu
cintad─лra n─лs─Уva s─Уyuс╣н─У kaladi …. iс╣Гta ..
upak─Бramuga d─Уha mosagiti viс╣нu n─Бku
upami├▒ci n─У j─Уs─Уpratyupak─Бra mika n─Уdi
yepuс╕Н┼л n─лdharmamuna niс╣нu n─лruс╣Зasthuс╕Нanai
prapannuс╕Нanai n─Уnu bradukuс╣н─У kaladi …. iс╣Гta ..
v─Уv─Уga veс╣Яс╣Яij─Уyaka viv─Уki j─Уsitivi

y─лvala n─лku g─лrtig─Б niс╣нс╣н─У n─лy─Бdh─лnuс╕Нanai

jaс╕Нulal┼Н g┼лrcaka y─Бc─Бryunil┼Н(t┼Н?) g┼лrcitivi
naс╕Нap─Ус╣нin─лsaraviki n─Бsaravi y─Уmunnadi

What else is there other than this? Even upon thinking!
To get rid of worries, serving You is the right way!
As a favor You gave me this body!
What can I do in return for it, befittingly?
At all times, being righteous and being indebted to You
happily if I live, that is the right way!
Not making me a fool, You made me a wise one!
For this, is there anything I can give in exchange?
Here, bringing You fame if I remain under Your control
and live without any fear, that is the right way!
Not letting me join the ignorant ones, You made me associate with Acharya!
For this noble deed of Yours, what can I give in return?
Without letting go, O SreeVenkatesha, being Your servant
if I live thus, that is the right way!!

I seek Your consent O Upendra! Now!
All this haste is but to serve You!
All that I see with my eyes, O Lotus eyed, it is Your divine feet
All that I hear, O Vishnu, are Your glories
All the right words that I speak, O Trivikrama, are Your incantations
All that I think of, I surrender it unto You!
Likewise, wherever I tread, O Hari, it is like circumambulating You
All my esoteric deeds, O Govinda, it is Your тАШKainkaryamтАЩ
All that I partake and eat, O Mukunda, it is Your prasadam
Without fail, all my comforts, under Your control I placed!
Wherever I lie down, O Lord of all, it is prostration unto You
All the thoughts that I think of, O Damodhara, it is contemplation on You
On all four sides, O SreeVenkatanayaka, it is but Your command
Totally my existence, I entrust unto You!!!

The one who desires and accepts saying тАШThis is what I wantтАЩ, he is the great one!
Do not let go, this is the philosophy of Hari-daasas, I shall now describe, O great ones!
To comprehend in the mind that God exists, that itself is the тАШJanma-PhalamuтАЩ1
Thinking about Him constantly is one’s fortune
To follow without fail the SreeVaishnava Dharma1 is true glory
Not differentiating between the deities is real virtue!
To abstain form Kaama3 and Krodha4 is an auspicious experience
Not committing sins knowingly is itself a gain
Living righteously and becoming dispassionate is itself pristine joy
Regularly engaging in the service of Acharya is accrued wealth!
Not falling in to the passions of nature is but being supremely Sattvik5
Shirking off all attachments is itself the Kingly post
Worshipping Alamelumanga and Her consort SreeVenkata Vibhu
as a pure hearted one, is itself eternal and highest glory!!
1.The fruit of life
2.The philosophy of Ramanujacharya
3.Desires
4.Anger
5.The mode of goodness

Sree VenkateshwaraтАЩs fascinating beauty if described
in whatever way we perceive, it matches these!
The hand that wields the Chakra which saved the elephant
to say that it is like an elephants trunk, is befitting
The Varada-Hasta1 that bestows boons
can be compared to a branch of the Kalpataru2 tree!
The hand that holds the Panchajanya which was born of the ocean
can be called as the wave of an ocean!
The Kati-Hasta3 which held the tail of the mighty Kalinga
can be agreeably praised as the king of snakes!
The chest that is in-between the two lotus like hands
can be called as the firm abode of Alamelumanga
You, who exist on the top of Venkatagiri
can be gloriously called as SreeVenkatesha!
1.Varada Hasta is the hand that bestows boons, held in a blessing posture
2.Kalpataru tree is a wish yielding tree
3.Kati Hasta is the hand that is placed on the waist

In this manner, may You shower Your grace!
Where else can we put forth our pleadings?
I contemplated on Your form, I touched Your feet
I joined the group of Your daasas
My sorrows trembled, my karmas became detached
About Your joyous glories, what more can I say?
I wore Your mudras, I praised Your attributes
With my hands I touched and worshipped Your Sree-Angas1
The Tamasik qualities dropped off, in a timely manner came Saatvik qualities
What more can we ask of You fondly?
I wore the Tiruman, I humbly took teertha and prasadam
I enjoyed listening to the many glorious stories of Yours
SreeVenkatesha! I could perceive тАШnowтАЩ and тАШhereafterтАЩ
Being totally satisfied, what else can we desire for?!

It is each ones fortune that is written on the forehead
With courage, do find out which is the superior one!!
Some saying тАШAll philosophies are oneтАЩ
raised and showed their Pattavardhanam1!
Like wise , some others, though saying тАШJangam is LingamтАЩ2
believe that birth itself is ashes, and smear it visibly!
Some saying тАШThere is nothing else except destruction at the endтАЩ
showed their empty forehead!
Some others, saying тАШThe Lord of Lakshmi is the AntaratmaтАЩ
applied the marks of Namam and Sreechoornam visibly!
Gloriously, Sree Venkatesha alone is the destiny,
He is the consort of Alamelumanga!
On this earth, these lines of fortune, He has written
only for those daasas who desired them!!

Purport :

Annamacharya says here that though there are several doctrines
existing, one must try to analyze the one that is closest to the truth. The followers
of Ramanuja, the Sree Vaishnavas, believe that the Lord is the innermost of all
Jivas and so He is the Supreme ruler who is to be served. Those who have
realized that Lord Vishnu is the supreme diety accept to become his тАШdasasтАЩ and
wear the marks of Tiruman - Sree choornam. They know that the consort of
Alamelumanga, Lord Sri Hari is the sole destiny. These lines of forture,
Annamayya says, have been written by the Lord himself for those who desired
it and not for everyone else.
1.Cloth worn on the forehead with titles imprinted on it.
2.Jangam is Lingam = The worshipper of the Linga becomes the Linga himself.

When the life force is at the roots, why water the top?
The great Lord is He, who is at the end as the ultimate fruit!
The sacrifices are Hari, the rites are Hari
For the Pithrus1, Hari alone is the great contentment
The essence of all eternal mantras is Hari
Serving Him alone, one attains all these fruits!

The Lord is Hari, our existence is but Hari
Constantly Hari alone is everything!
The eternal Time is SreeVenkatagiri Hari
On this earth, surrendering unto Him alone is fruitful!!!
The essence is that - By serving Hari alone, one can achieve all merits
attained by performing various other deeds.

Why that birth, which does not know of Hari?
What is the use of that study which does not concern Him?
Why the penance without compassion?
Why that devotion without any fear for God?
Why that dispute without love for others?
Why sing the praises of Lord when not living righteously?
Why perform the deeds that are fruitless?
Why so much pride without any wealth?
Why be adamant without a strong will?
Why possess a body that does not think of Showri1?
Why the rulership which is not befitting?
Why move about with anyone without affection for them?
Surrendering unto the matchless SreeVenkatesha,
if we can live, why then worry at all?
1. Lord Vishnu

For all those who are constantly engaged in worship, the Saguna form is the authority!
This manifested form which is worshipped by all sages, is alone the authority!
Some say You are тАШSagunaтАЩ, some say You are тАШNirgunaтАЩ
according to their knowledge acquired by various means, they argue amongst themselves!
Since You are immeasurable and autonomous, Valmiki, without saying anything else,
said тАЬNirgunaya GunatmaneтАЭ1, and this statement alone is the authority!!
тАЬSohamтАЭ said some people, тАЬDasohamтАЭ said some others
the two kinds of great expositions, which the wise ones praise!
Having borne a human body, saying тАЬDasohamтАЭ, Shuka attained You
The thought of тАЬSohamтАЭ, what proof did it give to the worlds??
Even by following the six shastras, the six mathas2, the six Karmas
without surrendering unto You, there is no other way!
Narada and other such devotees, having examined various other means
surrendered unto You, O Venkatapathi! That itself is the authority!!!
Purport: The Advaitins say that Brahman (Lord) is Nirguna, ie without any attributes, and
that the Jiva itself is the Paramatman-тАШSohamтАЩ.
The philosophy of Ramanuja (Visistadvaita) says that the Lord is full of auspicious attributes-
Saguna, and that the jiva is the Daasa of the Lord- Daasoham (I am Your Daasa).
Quoting form the scriptures, Annamayya says here that the path of Sharanagati unto the
Saguna form of the Lord, as taught by Ramanuja, is alone the right one!
1.Nirgunaya Gunatmane means : The one who is devoid of all evil qualities
and is the abode of numerous auspicious qualities.
2.The various philosophies

All these days, we were oblivious of You!
Today , He who cautioned me in my mind, He is Lord Vishnu!!
He nourishes as a Mother, protects as a Father
As one close to the heart, He rules over the body
As a giver He gently bestows, as a gentle lady He looks after
In all ways, He alone is our close relative, that Lord Vishnu!
He forgives as the Lord, as a dear one He advices
As a near one, He moves about closely
As a little boy He shows affection, as the life-force He resides within
In this manner, He alone is our close relative, that Lord Vishnu!
As a God He accepts worship, Being visibly present
on SreeVenkatadri, He bestows prosperity!
As an abode He grants refuge, as the thought He bestows fruits
Here and there, He alone is our close relative, that Lord Vishnu!!!

n─Бn─Бv─Уda┼Ы─Бstramulu navapur─Бс╣З─Уtih─Бsamulu

You alone are enough for me, O lotus eyed Narayana!
I have realized that You alone are the means, rest all is fruitless!
Pronouncing Your name alone is the remover of sorrows
Pronouncing Your name alone is the one that bestows auspiciousness
The various Vedas, Shastras, the nine Puranas, the Ithihasas
all exist within You name! Rest are all fruitless!
The origin of the sky, earth, and the nether worlds is but Your feet
The evolution of all Jivas originates from Your feet
The sentient beings, non sentient things, the divine beings, the sages,
and everything originate from Your feet alone! Rest are all fruitless!
O Lord, Your divine body is the means and support of the entire Universe
O Lord, Your divine body is the source of creation, sustenance and destruction
SreeVenkatapathi! I surrender my thoughts and my mind unto You
O Lord! I surrendered unto You! All other means are fruitless!!!

Whatever the ways of Kali yuga, there is always Your compassion!
O lotus eyed Hari! Hari, O Lord of all!
Whatever be the measure of the sin, to absolve it
with me is Your glorious name!
However much be the rage, to bestow peace
You exist within my mind!
On this earth, how much ever my senses chase me
to protect me, there is the path of Sharanagathi unto You!
To untie the binding ropes of great attachments due to Karmas
constantly, there is my devotion for You!
To bestow benevolently, all the desired things тАШhereтАЩ and тАШhereafterтАЩ
eternally, there is Your Sankirtanam!
To make my penances fruitful easily, O SreeVenkatesha
as тАШthe meansтАЩ, there is Your Kamala-devi1!
1. Godess Lakshmi, who is ever compassionate

O Parama Purusha! O matchless one!
I surrender unto You! O true abode of Lakshmi!
O one with a lotus navel! O lotus eyed!
O Lord with lotus like feet!
O Lord of all demigods and sages!
O lord of the herds! O granter of boons!
O four-formed one! O one with four arms!
O one who wields the conch and discus!
O Supreme Lord of Venkata Hill,
O enjoyer of the praises of Anjana!

dharal┼Н “nedbh─Бvaс╣Г tadbhavaтАЩтАЩ taneg─Бna
harimayam─У jagamant─Бnu …. dharal┼Н ..
mahi n┼Нdaс╣нiv─Бrandu malinamu dalacina
tahataha manas─У t─Б malinamu
vahi nediс╣нandu bh─Бvanamu bh─Бvi├▒cina

yekkuva nediс╣нip─Бp─Б le├▒ci nindic─Ус╣нi -

On this earth, it is тАЬYath Bhaavam тАУ Tad BhavathiтАЭ1
Hari alone pervades the whole world!
In this world, if one thinks others to be sinful
that kind of a mind itself is sinful!
In the same way, if one thinks that others are good
in very many ways, that person alone is good!
If one tries to criticize the sinful ways of others
such an ignorant tongue is itself worthy of blame!
Seeing only the meritorious deeds of others, if one praises them to be great
such a virtuous tongue is itself great!
Constantly if one seeks the Saguna form of SreeVenkatapathi,
the Jiva who knows the essence of it, is himself full of qualities!
Out of cleverness, if one thinks of Him as Nirguna,
Such a person without any difference, he himself becomes devoid of all qualities!
1.Literally means: тАЬwhat one thinks of, that alone he becomesтАЭ
The final purport is that what one thinks of, he himself becomes that.
So he who thinks that the Lord is devoid of qualities, himself becomes
devoid of all qualities!!

For everything, Hari тАУ the Antaryami, is the origin
All other means that are heard of, or seen, are fruitless!
For Moksha, joyful тАШVairagyaтАЩ1 is the origin
For strong attachments, Samsara is the origin
For happiness, Supreme peace is the origin
For extreme sorrow, excessive rage is the origin
For all the sorrows that we accrue, Our Karma is the origin
For Supreme bliss, devotion to Sree-Kantha is the origin
For contemplation, thought is the origin
For attachments, body is the origin
For attaining the rare right-knowledge, Acharya is the origin
On this earth, for the material world, money is the origin
For supreme salvation, SreeVenkatapathi is the origin
For me, Sharanagathi unto Hari is the supreme means!

Because of Him alone, here on this earth there is prosperity!

┼Ыr─лv─Ус╣Еkaс╣н─Бdrim─лdi ┼Ыr─лnarasiс╣Гh─Б sarva
j─лvaday─Бparuс╕Нa v┼Н ┼Ыr─лnarasiс╣Гh─Б …. c─Уpaс╣нс╣нi ..
Holding us, do protect us, Sree Narasimha
Your тАШSree PaadasтАЩ are the only means, Sree Narasimha
You are splendid with a thousand arms, Sree Narasimha
With benevolent smiles, Sree Narasimha
Flawless You are, O glorious Sree Narasimha
You placed Your beloved on your thigh, Sree Narasimha!
O one like the milky ocean, Sree Narasimha
O one with strong nails that tore open the demons, Sree Narasimha
O one who blessed Prahalada, Sree Narasimha
The devathas praise You, O Sree Narasimha!
You reside with Goddess Sree, Sree Narasimha
Valorous are Your deeds, Sree Narasimha
You who reside on Sree Venkatadri, Sree Narasimha
O one who is full of compassion towards all Jivas, Sree Narasimha!!

We cannot think of ourselves as Brahman!
We do not even have the independence that we desire!
To create, in a moment, the multitude of all Jivas
there is one who exists separately!
The one who exists in the most subtle to the highest as the тАШAntaryaminтАЩ
To Him we offer our worship and exist as His daasas!
Perceivable to Brahma and other Gods, to rule over autonomously
there is one who exists separately!
He is that one who is the prosperous Lord of Lakshmi
We exist as those who work as ordained by Him!
Being the eternal protector, being the wielder of the Shanka-Chakra
there exists Sree Venkatapathi , separately as the Lord!
Coming unto His fold, with joyful ecstasy,
in a matchless way, we live amongst all !!!

n─Бс╣нiki n─Бс╕Н─У n─Б caduvu
m─Бс╣нal─Бс╕Нucunu maс╣Яac─Ус╣нi caduvu …. n─Бс╣нiki ..
enaya n─лtani neс╣Яuguс╣нak─У p┼Н

sirula nitani maс╣Яaceс╕Нi korak─У p┼Н

My daily studies are but for the day!
Even as I utter anything, I tend to forget such studies!
The people in the past studied
only to understand Him!
While the egoistic people of today engage in studies
only to forget Him!
In the earlier Yugas like the Kruta-Yuga, though He was known
yet the studies were only to know Him fully!
In the kali-Yuga, though He exists for us,
the studies are only to deny His presence!
Lords like Brahma and others engage in studies
only to perceive Lord TiruVenkatapathi as the Supreme!
Being affluent, the academic studies of materialistic Jivas
are only to forget Him!!

What more can You do, O Lord? You are the treasury of compassion!
For those who are unable to comprehend, it is their ill-luck !
тАЬI shall bestow Parama Pada1 by destroying the sinsтАЭ
Thus You proclaimed in the тАШCharama SlokaтАЩ2 at the very beginning
Eternally on this earth, from Your side there are no shortcomings
It is the ill-luck of those who lack total faith in You!
The loving relationship between Your feet and me, in a supreme manner
You proclaimed it as the essence of the Dvayam3 at the very beginning
If rightly appraised, from Your side there is no fault
It is the ill-luck of those who do not believe!
In the many Puranas, declaring тАЬI am easily attainable by BhaktasтАЭ
O inner self, You spoke thus at the very beginning
O Venkatesha! What more can You do?
It is the ill-luck of the adamant people who lack faith!
1.Parama Padam : The Supreme Realm
2.Charama Sloka : The 66th verse of chapter 18 of Bagavad Gita
3.Dvayam : The Dvaya mantra which shows the relationship between God
and the Jiva to be that of a Lord and servant
